\DoxyCodeLine{00624\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Estimation\ of\ number\ of\ circle\ segment\ based\ on\ error\ is\ derived\ using\ method\ described\ in\ https://stackoverflow.com/a/2244088/15194693}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00625\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Number\ of\ segments\ (N)\ is\ calculated\ using\ equation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00626\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ N\ =\ ceil\ (\ pi\ /\ acos(1\ -\/\ error\ /\ r)\ )\ \ \ \ \ where\ r\ >\ 0,\ error\ <=\ r}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00627\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Our\ equation\ is\ significantly\ simpler\ that\ one\ in\ the\ post\ thanks\ for\ choosing\ segment\ that\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00628\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ perpendicular\ to\ X\ axis.\ Follow\ steps\ in\ the\ article\ from\ this\ starting\ condition\ and\ you\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00629\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ will\ get\ this\ result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00630\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00631\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Rendering\ circles\ with\ an\ odd\ number\ of\ segments,\ while\ mathematically\ correct\ will\ produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00632\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ asymmetrical\ results\ on\ the\ raster\ grid.\ Therefore\ we're\ rounding\ N\ to\ next\ even\ number\ (7-\/>8,\ 8-\/>8,\ 9-\/>10\ etc.)}}
